# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Firefox CSS Style Resolution to Layout Paint Chain

## Your Task

Trace how a CSS style change triggers layout and paint in mozilla/gecko-dev. Find C++ source files implementing: the style change notification, the frame style recomputation, the dirty-frame reflow scheduling, the display list construction, and the WebRender layer update.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the crossrepo domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/firefox--871325b8.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/firefox--871325b8` (mozilla-firefox/firefox)

Create a file at `/workspace/answer.json` with your findings in the following structure:

```json

}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

## Summary

I've traced the complete pipeline showing how a CSS style change triggers layout and paint in mozilla/gecko-dev:

### Key Files Identified:

1. **Style Change Notification** - `RestyleManager`, `ServoStyleSet`, `GeckoBindings`
2. **Frame Style Recomputation** - Style computation through Servo engine
3. **Dirty Frame Reflow Scheduling** - `PresShell::FrameNeedsReflow()`, dirty frame tracking
4. **Display List Construction** - `nsDisplayListBuilder`, `RetainedDisplayListBuilder`
5. **WebRender Layer Update** - `WebRenderLayerManager`, `RenderRootStateManager`

### The Complete Chain:

```
PostRestyleEvent() 
  → ServoStyleSet (style computation)
  → ProcessRestyledFrames() (apply change hints)
  → FrameNeedsReflow() (mark frames dirty)
  → DoReflow() (layout calculation)
  → BuildDisplayList() (create visual items)
  → RetainedDisplayListBuilder (optimize)
  → WebRenderLayerManager (GPU commands)
  → WebRenderBridgeChild (send to GPU)
```

The answer includes all relevant C++ source files, key classes/functions, and a detailed narrative explaining how each component works together to handle CSS style changes from initial notification through final GPU rendering.

complete pipeline of how a CSS style change triggers layout and paint in the Firefox/Gecko browser engine.\\n\\n### 1. Style Change Notification\\n\\nThe process begins when a style change is detected (via attribute changes, class changes, or direct style modifications):\\n\\n- **Entry Point**: `layout/base/nsLayoutUtils.cpp:PostRestyleEvent()` - This is the public API that posts restyle events for elements that have changed style.\\n- **Core Handler**: `layout/style/RestyleManager.h` and `layout/style/RestyleManager.cpp` - The RestyleManager class is responsible for managing the restyling process. It receives change notifications through `PostRestyleEvent(Element*, RestyleHint, nsChangeHint)`.\\n- **Context**: `layout/base/nsPresContext.h` and `.cpp` - The nsPresContext owns the RestyleManager and coordinates the overall presentation.\\n\\n### 2. Frame Style Recomputation\\n\\nOnce restyle events are posted, they are processed during a flush:\\n\\n- **Style Computation**: `layout/style/ServoStyleSet.h` and `layout/style/ServoStyleSet.cpp` - ServoStyleSet performs the actual style computation using the Servo CSS engine. It computes new styles for elements based on CSS rules and cascade.\\n- **Gecko Bindings**: `layout/style/GeckoBindings.cpp` - Bridges between the Servo style engine and Gecko layout code. Functions like `Gecko_ElementStateChanged()` notify Gecko when element state changes require restyling.\\n- **Change Hints**: `layout/style/nsChangeHint.h` - Defines nsChangeHint flags that specify what layout work is needed (reflow, repaint, etc.) based on the style change.\\n- **Restyle State**: The `ServoRestyleState` class in `layout/style/RestyleManager.h` manages the state during the restyle traversal, including tracking which frames need work.\\n\\n### 3. Dirty Frame Reflow Scheduling\\n\\nAfter styles are recomputed, frames are marked dirty and reflow is scheduled:\\n\\n- **Restyle Processing**: `layout/style/RestyleManager.cpp:ProcessRestyledFrames()` - This function processes the list of elements that were restyled, examines their change hints, and marks frames dirty accordingly. It iterates through the style change list and applies the necessary frame updates.\\n- **Frame Marking**: `layout/base/PresShell.h` and `layout/base/PresShell.cpp:FrameNeedsReflow()` - This method marks a frame and its ancestors as needing reflow by setting dirty bits (NS_FRAME_IS_DIRTY, NS_FRAME_HAS_DIRTY_CHILDREN). It also adds the frame to the dirty roots list for reflow scheduling.\\n- **Reflow Scheduling**: `layout/generic/nsIFrame.h` - The nsIFrame base class manages frame state bits that track dirty status. Ancestors are marked with NS_FRAME_HAS_DIRTY_CHILDREN to propagate the need for reflow up the tree.\\n- **Flush Mechanism**: `layout/base/PresShell.cpp:FlushPendingNotifications()` and `DoFlushPendingNotifications()` - These methods coordinate the flushing of different types of pending notifications (style, frames, layout). They ensure the restyle and reflow happen in the correct order.\\n\\n### 4. Display List Construction\\n\\nDuring reflow, the display list is rebuilt to represent what needs to be painted:\\n\\n- **Reflow Execution**: `layout/base/PresShell.cpp:DoReflow()` - Performs the actual reflow by calling frame's Reflow() methods. This recalculates sizes and positions.\\n- **Display List Building**: `layout/painting/nsDisplayList.h` and `layout/painting/nsDisplayList.cpp:nsDisplayListBuilder` - The nsDisplayListBuilder constructs the display list by traversing the frame tree. It builds display items that represent visual content in z-order.\\n- **Frame Traversal**: Frames' `BuildDisplayList()` methods are called recursively to build display items. Each frame contributes its own display items (backgrounds, borders, content, etc.).\\n- **Retained Display Lists**: `layout/painting/RetainedDisplayListBuilder.h` and `layout/painting/RetainedDisplayListBuilder.cpp` - Optimizes display list building by retaining and reusing parts of the previous display list when possible, only rebuilding changed portions.\\n- **Display List Processing**: The built display list is then used for painting. It contains all the visual elements in the correct z-order and clipping information needed for rendering.\\n\\n### 5. WebRender Layer Update\\n\\nFinally, the display list is converted to WebRender commands for GPU-accelerated rendering:\\n\\n- **Layer Manager**: `gfx/layers/wr/WebRenderLayerManager.h` and `gfx/layers/wr/WebRenderLayerManager.cpp` - The WebRenderLayerManager is the compositor abstraction that manages the rendering pipeline. It converts the display list into WebRender display list format.\\n- **State Management**: `gfx/layers/wr/RenderRootStateManager.h` - Manages the WebRender state for a render root, handling display items and WebRender commands.\\n- **Bridge Communication**: `gfx/layers/wr/WebRenderBridgeChild.h` and `gfx/layers/wr/WebRenderBridgeChild.cpp` - Communicates with the WebRender bridge parent process, sending the display list and resource updates.\\n- **Transaction**: The display list is wrapped in a WebRender transaction that updates the WebRender scene. This includes creating WebRender display list items, handling scrolling data, and managing layer properties.\\n- **GPU Rendering**: WebRender processes these commands on the GPU, performing composition, rasterization, and other rendering operations.\\n\\n### Summary of the Chain\\n\\nThe complete flow is:\\n\\n1. Style change detected \u2192 **PostRestyleEvent()** (nsLayoutUtils, RestyleManager)\\n2. Style recomputed \u2192 **ServoStyleSet** processes styles, determines **nsChangeHint**\\n3. Frames marked dirty \u2192 **ProcessRestyledFrames()** applies hints, **FrameNeedsReflow()** schedules reflow\\n4. Reflow executed \u2192 **DoReflow()** recalculates layout\\n5. Display list built \u2192 **nsDisplayListBuilder::BuildDisplayList()** and **RetainedDisplayListBuilder** create visual representation\\n6. WebRender updated \u2192 **WebRenderLayerManager** converts to WebRender commands, **WebRenderBridgeChild** sends to GPU\\n\\nThis pipeline ensures that CSS style changes efficiently propagate through the layout engine to the GPU for rendering.\"\n}\n",
